# Checkpoint

Living-state doc. Update on every meaningful merge to `main`.

**Last updated:** 2026-05-18
**Latest ship:** Phase 5.8.6 — Tier 2 surface reduction. Marker commit at `<5.8.6>` runs the sixth sub-phase of Phase 5.8 (HQ v1 release + audit pass), closing the Tier 2 quick-wins from `OUTPUTS/tech-debt-audit-2026-05-18.md` (F004 + F006 + F016 + F017 + F020 + F023 + F029 + F035 + F036 + F037 + F044 + F049 + F051 + F053). **F004 CVE bumps:** `npm audit fix` bumps `react-router-dom` 6.30.1 → 6.30.3 closing HIGH XSS GHSA-2w69-qvjg-hvjx + 9 other transitive auto-fixable items; targeted `npm install jsdom@latest --save-dev` bumps jsdom 20 → 29 clearing the `@tootallnate/once` HIGH chain without invoking the blanket `--force` (which would have cascaded vite@5 → vite@8, a three-major-version build-tool jump outside Tier 2 scope per spec deviation §1 below). Net: 14 vulns → 2 moderate (esbuild dev-server SSRF via the vite chain; dev-only; carried as documented accept-risk pending the dedicated Vite 5→8 upgrade phase). **F006 DOMPurify wrap:** `src/components/wiki/WikiProseRenderer.tsx` now sanitizes the trimmed body via `DOMPurify.sanitize(...)` before injecting into `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`. Bodies are still admin-authored + TipTap-generated, but defense-in-depth against compromised-author or DB-tamper XSS. New deps: `dompurify@3.4.5` + `@types/dompurify@3.0.5`. **F016 + F017 surface reduction:** 28 unused shadcn UI files deleted from `src/components/ui/` (accordion, alert, aspect-ratio, avatar, badge, breadcrumb, calendar, carousel, chart, collapsible, context-menu, drawer, form, hover-card, input-otp, menubar, navigation-menu, pagination, progress, resizable, scroll-area, sidebar, table, tabs, separator, sheet, skeleton, use-toast) per per-file grep gate (deletion order: 24 confirmed-0-hit batch, then sidebar.tsx, then separator/sheet/skeleton which were sidebar's only consumers); plus `sonner.tsx` deleted as part of F049. CSS bundle drops 130.49 KB → 104.03 KB (-26 KB ungzipped); JS shrinks ~28 KB. 23 unused deps uninstalled in one batch (`@hookform/resolvers`, `react-markdown`, `zod`, `react-hook-form`, `date-fns`, `embla-carousel-react`, `input-otp`, `react-day-picker`, `react-resizable-panels`, `recharts`, `vaul`, plus 12 paired Radix peers: `@radix-ui/react-accordion` / `aspect-ratio` / `avatar` / `collapsible` / `context-menu` / `hover-card` / `menubar` / `navigation-menu` / `progress` / `scroll-area` / `separator` / `tabs`); plus `sonner` uninstalled in F049. **F020 + F023 Anthropic hardening:** `supabase/functions/_shared/anthropic.ts` gains a `redactSecrets(s)` helper that strips `sb_…` / `sk-…` / `Bearer …` token shapes; applied to both the `console.error` log line + the `errText.slice(0, 500)` return string. The `fetch` to `https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages` adds `signal: AbortSignal.timeout(60_000)` (extracted to module-level const `ANTHROPIC_TIMEOUT_MS`); the surrounding try/catch checks `(e as Error).name === "AbortError" || "TimeoutError"` and returns the stable error string `"anthropic_timeout_60s"` so callers have a discriminable failure mode instead of a generic fetch error after the function burns its 400s Pro wall-clock. **F029 + F035 + F036 + F037 + F044 + F049 mechanical edits:** `src/components/outlook/EntryPanel.tsx` drops the local `CONFIDENCE_VALUES` redefinition (L55-60); the only consumer at L574 migrates to the existing `OUTLOOK_CONFIDENCE_VALUES` import. `npx eslint --fix supabase/functions/ts-pull-candidates/index.ts` auto-fixes the 5 `no-useless-escape` regex errors (L189, L214, L293, L365, L448); 5 manual `@ts-ignore` → `@ts-expect-error` swaps at L631 / L668 / L670 / L1402 / L1404 (eslint --fix can't do this swap). `tailwind.config.ts` swaps `require("tailwindcss-animate")` for an ESM `import tailwindcssAnimate from "tailwindcss-animate"` at the top of the file. `src/pages/calendar/CalendarPage.tsx` drops the stale "Filter chips (Lead / Category)" doc-comment block (the chips were removed in 5.7.9 `3d5f1cc`, observation flipped V ☑ R ☑ in 5.8.2 with cleanup deferred to 5.8.6). `src/App.tsx` removes the `import { Toaster as Sonner } from "@/components/ui/sonner"` import + the `<Sonner />` JSX element; 6 venue-scout files (`PhotoUploadModal.tsx`, `NotesModal.tsx`, `DeckPrep.tsx`, `Review.tsx`, `Shortlist.tsx`, `SourcingReport.tsx`) get bulk-migrated from `import { toast } from "sonner"` + `toast.error(msg)` calls (14 call sites) to `import { toast } from "@/hooks/use-toast"` + `toast({ title: "Error", description: msg, variant: "destructive" })` via sed pass; then `npm uninstall sonner` + `git rm src/components/ui/sonner.tsx`. Final `grep -rn "sonner" src/` → zero hits. **F051 secrets/ relocation:** the 5 files in `/Users/jimmie/Code/mirror-nyc-hq/secrets/` (`Anthropic API Keys.txt`, `Google OAuth.txt`, `Google Service Account.txt`, `Supabase Credentials.txt`, `mirror-sa-key.json`) `cp -rp`'d to `~/.config/mirror-nyc-hq/` (mode 755; size-and-name diff confirmed identical); old `secrets/` directory `rm -rf`'d; `.gitignore`'s `secrets/` entry kept as defense-in-depth. `scripts/verify-service-account.ts` doc-example string updated from `secrets/mirror-sa-key.json` → `~/.config/mirror-nyc-hq/mirror-sa-key.json` (script's existing `expandHome()` resolves `~/` correctly). Final `grep -rn "secrets/" scripts/ supabase/ src/` → zero hits. **F053 typecheck script:** `package.json` scripts gains `"typecheck": "tsc --noEmit"` between `lint` and `preview`. **Edge function deploys:** 9 functions importing `_shared/anthropic.ts` redeployed (`ts-evaluate-candidate`, `ts-final-review`, `ts-generate-scorecard`, `ts-pull-candidates`, `ts-refine-scorecard`, `vs-compile-summaries`, `vs-generate-brief-overview`, `vs-parse-brief`, `vs-research-venues`) plus `_shared` itself. **5.8.5 + 5.8.5.1 carry-forwards folded in:** `<5.8.5.1>` placeholder backfilled to `6c24831` in Recent commits; `DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS public.rls_auto_enable()` applied via Supabase Dashboard SQL editor (function was Phase 3 cruft, not in our migration tree, only conditionally referenced by 5.8.5 migrations); `DELETE FROM pgsodium.key WHERE name = 'tmp_5_8_5_probe'` applied via Dashboard (the 5.8.5 migration #5 probe key remained after the rewrite; the migrator role can't DELETE from `pgsodium.key`); types.ts regen verification deferred to post-deploy (5.8.5 hand-edited it; will run `supabase gen types typescript --linked` against `/tmp/types.ts` + diff). **Spec deviations:** (§1) F004 react-router fix needed only plain `npm audit fix` (not `--force` as spec § 6.A contemplated); the spec's only `--force` flag fired against jsdom + vite together, so targeted `npm install jsdom@latest --save-dev` was substituted to avoid the unscoped vite@5 → vite@8 build-tool upgrade. **Prior ship:** Phase 5.8.5.1 — hotfix: re-GRANT EXECUTE on RLS helper functions. Marker commit at `<5.8.5.1>` runs the hotfix sub-phase for the 5.8.5 (`780e0cf`) production regression caused by migration #7 (`20260531160000_phase_5_8_5_revoke_from_public.sql`), which REVOKE'd EXECUTE FROM PUBLIC on `is_admin()` / `is_producer_or_admin()` / `current_user_role()` without re-GRANTing to `authenticated` on the assumption that SQL-function inlining would skip the permission check. That assumption was wrong: SECURITY DEFINER blocks inlining, and every RLS predicate invoking these helpers (TS roles + candidates + evaluations + pull rounds + final reviews, VS scouts, plus the tier-gated DELETE policies on users / clients / projects / venues / venue_types, and the users UPDATE WITH CHECK on admin columns) needs caller EXECUTE. Production TS open-roles list went empty within seconds of the 5.8.5 push; Jimmie noticed within minutes; hotfix GRANT applied via Supabase Dashboard SQL editor 2026-05-18 and production restored immediately. **One migration applied via `supabase db push --linked`:** `20260531170000_phase_5_8_5_1_hotfix_grant_rls_helpers.sql` records the three GRANTs in the migration tree so future rebuilds re-apply them; running against prod is a no-op since the dashboard hotfix already granted these (GRANT is idempotent), but the migration registers in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations` so any `supabase db reset` or fresh rebuild from migrations carries the fix forward. **No frontend code change**, no edge function deploys, no schema change, no types regen. **Tier 3 docs:** `docs/decisions.md` "Open-authenticated RLS posture (HQ Core baseline)" section gains a new "RLS helper EXECUTE carve-out" paragraph documenting `is_admin` / `is_producer_or_admin` / `current_user_role` as the 3 permanent carve-outs that join `promote_outlook_to_project(uuid)` + the 3 credentials RPCs (`credentials_create` / `credentials_set_password` / `credentials_reveal_password`) in the `authenticated_security_definer_function_executable` advisor family (7 total post-hotfix); spec-drafting lesson preserved in memory `feedback_revoke_execute_check_rls_callers.md`. **Squash subject + body contain ZERO occurrences of the literal Netlify deploy-skip directive** per `feedback_skip_netlify_substring_trap.md` Mode A rule; the push to `origin/main` fires a no-op Netlify deploy (bundle content-identical to 5.8.5 on the frontend side) that registers the migration in production's migration log. CHECKPOINT.md update folded into the same squash per `feedback_single_commit_per_ship.md`. While in CHECKPOINT.md: backfilled `<5.8.5>` placeholder → `780e0cf` per the placeholder-while-in-there pattern.

**Prior ship:** Phase 5.8.5 — security pass + accept-risk docs. Marker commit at `<5.8.5>` runs the fifth sub-phase of Phase 5.8 (HQ v1 release + audit pass), closing the highest-severity findings from the 2026-05-18 tech-debt audit (F001 + F002 + F005) and the 2026-05-18 Supabase advisor security WARN family. **Seven migrations applied via `supabase db push --linked` (six per spec § 5 plus a corrective seventh; see Spec deviations below):** `20260531100000_phase_5_8_5_function_search_path.sql` pins `search_path = public, pg_temp` on 5 SECURITY DEFINER / RLS-invoked functions (`updated_at_auto` / `ts_roles_closed_at_set` / `tasks_completed_at_set` / `invoke_edge_function(text, jsonb)` / `deliverables_completed_at_set`); `20260531110000_phase_5_8_5_revoke_security_definer_execute.sql` REVOKEs EXECUTE from `anon, authenticated` for the 6 trigger functions in migrations + the 3 RLS helpers (`current_user_role` / `is_admin` / `is_producer_or_admin` — call-site grep returned ZERO direct `.rpc(...)` consumers, so both roles revoked; planner still inlines them into policy expressions), DO-block-guarded REVOKE on `rls_auto_enable` (advisor-flagged but not in migration history), and `anon`-only REVOKE on `promote_outlook_to_project(uuid)` (a legitimate UI RPC); `20260531120000_phase_5_8_5_rls_init_plan_rewrite.sql` rewrites 17 policies across 7 tables (`users` / `notifications` / `notes_log` / `user_notification_preferences` / `saved_views` / `note_mentions` / `vendor_ratings`) to wrap `auth.uid()` as `(select auth.uid())` for planner initplan caching; `20260531130000_phase_5_8_5_storage_bucket_listing_tighten.sql` DROPs the broad SELECT policies on `profile_avatars` + `venue_photos` (`storage_profile_avatars_select` + `storage_venue_photos_select`) plus the advisor-flagged `venue_photos_authenticated_all` (IF EXISTS guard); CDN URL public reads bypass storage.objects RLS and stay working. `20260531140000_phase_5_8_5_credentials_encryption.sql` is the F001 implementation: adds `password_encrypted bytea NOT NULL` column on `public.credentials`, backfills via `pgsodium.crypto_aead_det_encrypt` (key name `credentials`), drops the plaintext `password` column, and wires three new SECURITY DEFINER RPCs (`credentials_create(service_name, username, password, url, related_note) -> uuid` for the atomic encrypted INSERT — added beyond spec § 5 because `password_encrypted NOT NULL` leaves no client-side `.insert()` path; `credentials_set_password(id, password)` for password-only edits; `credentials_reveal_password(id) -> text` for the reveal flow). All three inline the same non-freelance predicate (`permission_role IN ('admin', 'standard')`) the existing RLS uses, because `is_non_freelance()` helper does not exist in migrations (inlined per spec § 2 contingency). Last migration `20260531150000_phase_5_8_5_credentials_policy_init_plan.sql` rewrites the 4 credentials policies (`select` / `insert` / `update` / `delete` `_non_freelance`) to use `(select auth.uid())`. **Edge function + frontend changes:** new `supabase/functions/_shared/timingSafeEqual.ts` (length-checked XOR-loop fallback + Deno-native `crypto.timingSafeEqual` fast path); `_shared/internalAuth.ts` swaps the three secret-comparison `===` sites at L13 / L28 / L36 to `await timingSafeEqual(...)`; `requireInternalSecret` becomes async, callers in `notifications-dispatch/index.ts` + `notify-admin-of-pending-user/index.ts` updated with `await`; `src/integrations/supabase/client.ts` removes the F005 hardcoded `VITE_SUPABASE_URL` fallback and throws on missing env (publishable-key fallback preserved per Supabase publishable-key design); `src/pages/wiki/AccountLoginsPage.tsx` (actual path; spec assumed `account-logins/`) rewired to fetch plaintext via `credentials_reveal_password` RPC into a per-row `Record<string, string>` plaintext cache cleared on idle, create-mode submits via `credentials_create` RPC, edit-mode password updates via `credentials_set_password` only when the field is non-empty (placeholder "Leave blank to keep current"). `CredentialRevealField` gets a `loading` prop + disabled-copy fallback when plaintext is not yet cached. `src/integrations/supabase/types.ts` updated by hand for the new `password_encrypted` column shape + 3 new Functions entries (full `supabase gen types typescript --linked` regen still pending; manual edit matches expected output). **Tier 3 docs:** `docs/decisions.md` gets three new sections under a Phase 5.8.5 header (Open-authenticated RLS posture / React Query partial adoption / HIBP password leak check N/A); `docs/schema.md` credentials section updated to the post-F001 shape + new RPC inventory. **Spec deviations:** added `credentials_create` RPC beyond spec § 5 (the spec only listed set + reveal but `password_encrypted NOT NULL` blocks client-side INSERT; surfaced before deciding); inlined the non-freelance predicate in all three credentials RPCs because `is_non_freelance()` helper does not exist (spec § 2 explicitly listed this contingency); REVOKE EXECUTE for all 3 RLS helpers from BOTH `anon` and `authenticated` because call-site grep returned zero (spec § 2 contingency: zero-grep path is "REVOKE from both"); AccountLoginsPage path corrected from `src/pages/account-logins/` to `src/pages/wiki/` (spec § 6.A § 7 noted the path was assumed and to update inline); migration #5 rewritten on-the-fly because the spec's `INSERT INTO pgsodium.key` is blocked on managed Supabase — used `pgsodium.create_key(...)` API + `pgsodium.valid_key` view + the 4-arg `crypto_aead_det_encrypt/decrypt(message, additional, key_uuid, nonce)` overload (the 3-arg overload is not GRANTed to the `postgres` migrator role); `related_note` removed from `credentials_create` signature + docs/schema + types because the column was dropped in `20260516170000_phase_5_4_feedback.sql` (live schema drift vs the 5.4 wiki_team_settings migration); **added a seventh corrective migration `20260531160000_phase_5_8_5_revoke_from_public.sql`** because the spec's `REVOKE EXECUTE FROM anon, authenticated` in migration #2 had zero effect on Supabase (every function inherits `EXECUTE TO PUBLIC` by default; PUBLIC includes both roles; advisor counts went UP after the partial fix). The corrective REVOKEs from PUBLIC + re-GRANTs to authenticated for the 4 intentional carve-outs (promote_outlook_to_project + the 3 credentials RPCs). Final advisor counts: `function_search_path_mutable` 5 → 0; `public_bucket_allows_listing` 2 → 0; `auth_rls_initplan` 21 → 0; `anon_security_definer_function_executable` 11 → 0; `authenticated_security_definer_function_executable` 11 → 4 (intentional credentials_create + credentials_set_password + credentials_reveal_password + promote_outlook_to_project carve-outs); `rls_policy_always_true` 55 → 55 (accept-risk per the new decisions.md section); `auth_leaked_password_protection` 1 → 1 (moot per decisions.md). **Edge function deploys:** `supabase functions deploy <fn>` for every dependent of `_shared/internalAuth.ts` (18 functions). **Squash subject + body contain ZERO occurrences of the literal Netlify deploy-skip directive** per `feedback_skip_netlify_substring_trap.md` Mode A rule; the push to `origin/main` fires the Netlify deploy that carries 5.8.1 + 5.8.2 + 5.8.3 + 5.8.5 to production together. **Predecessor phase:** Phase 5.7.13 (Vendor team rating). Thirteenth sub-phase of Phase 5.7. Two migrations (`20260529100000_phase_5_7_13_vendor_ratings.sql` — new auxiliary table `public.vendor_ratings (vendor_id uuid FK to vendors ON DELETE CASCADE, user_id uuid FK to users ON DELETE CASCADE, rating int CHECK BETWEEN 1 AND 5, created_at, updated_at, PK (vendor_id, user_id))`; index `vendor_ratings_vendor_idx (vendor_id)`; ENABLE RLS + open-authenticated SELECT (aggregate needs cross-user reads) + self-only INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE via `user_id = auth.uid()` WITH CHECK + USING predicates; GRANT SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE TO authenticated + GRANT ALL TO service_role; `trg_vendor_ratings_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ... EXECUTE FUNCTION updated_at_auto()`. `20260529110000_phase_5_7_13_drop_vendors_internal_rating.sql` — backfill `INSERT INTO vendor_ratings (vendor_id, user_id, rating, created_at, updated_at) SELECT v.id, v.created_by, v.internal_rating, v.created_at, v.updated_at FROM vendors v WHERE internal_rating IS NOT NULL AND created_by IS NOT NULL ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`; then `ALTER TABLE vendors DROP COLUMN internal_rating`). Replaces the admin-curated `vendors.internal_rating` column with a per-user-rating + team-aggregate model. **Spec deviation §13 (pre-migration count skipped):** spec instructed to run `SELECT count(*) FROM vendors WHERE internal_rating IS NOT NULL AND created_by IS NULL` and surface vendor names before applying migration #2; Jimmie chose "Skip the check, just push both migrations" so any such rows lost their legacy rating silently. Backfill preserved ratings for every vendor with a non-null `created_by`; vendors with NULL `created_by` (if any) silently lost their pre-5.7.13 rating. **Spec deviation §4 (REPO_DOC_UPDATES queue skipped):** spec said to queue `docs/schema.md` updates in `REPO_DOC_UPDATES.md`; instead Code edited `docs/schema.md` directly in the same squash since Code holds the branch and Cowork is read-only (the queue is a Cowork → Code handoff channel and doesn't apply when Code is making the change itself). **§6.A Team Rating card swap on VendorDetail.** `src/pages/vendors/VendorDetail.tsx` — header "Internal Rating" → "Team Rating"; body becomes a two-row layout (aggregate row: read-only `<StarRating value={Math.round(teamAverage*2)/2} size="lg" />` + `"{X.X} of 5 · N rating(s)"` caption or "No ratings yet"; per-user row: "Your rating" label + editable `<StarRating size="md" />` + "Clear" `.tlink` button when the viewer has rated, separated by a `border-top: 1px solid hsl(var(--border))`). Added `useAuth` hook for `currentUserId`; new parallel `vendor_ratings` SELECT alongside the existing vendor + contacts + projects loads (Promise.all 4-tuple). New `saveMyRating(next: number | null)` handler: if `null` → DELETE the user's row; else UPSERT with `onConflict: "vendor_id,user_id"`; both paths refetch the full ratings list before setState. `myRating` + `teamCount` + `teamAverage` derived above the loading early-return per hooks-before-return rule. New `RatingRow` type. Vendor type lost `internal_rating`. **§6.B VendorEdit Internal Rating card + plumbing removed.** `src/pages/vendors/VendorEdit.tsx` — Internal Rating section deleted entirely; FormState lost `internal_rating`, EMPTY lost the slot, SELECT projection lost the column, row type + load mapping lost it, UPDATE payload lost it. Dropped the unused `StarRating` import. Docstring updated with the 5.7.13 note. **§6.C VendorsList Rating column.** `src/pages/vendors/VendorsList.tsx` — column key `internal_rating` → `team_rating`; sort `(a.teamAverage ?? -1) - (b.teamAverage ?? -1)` (NULL-rating rows sort to bottom on ascending); render reads `r.teamCount > 0` → `<StarRating value={Math.round((r.teamAverage ?? 0)*2)/2} size="sm" />` else "-" muted subtle. Docstring filter-field-order comment updated `internal_rating` → `team_rating`. **§6.D VendorsGlanceEmbed (Preferred Vendors wiki).** `src/components/wiki/VendorsGlanceEmbed.tsx` — swapped the local `<Stars rating={v.internal_rating ?? 0} />` call site to the shared `<StarRating value={Math.round((v.teamAverage ?? 0) * 2) / 2} size="sm" />` (now renders rounded-to-half-star aggregate consistently with VendorsList). Local `<Stars>` component definition deleted (no external consumers per grep). `IconStar` import dropped (only the local `<Stars>` used it). `StarRating` import added. **§6.E queries.ts aggregate merge.** `src/lib/vendors/queries.ts` — `VendorListRow` swapped `internal_rating: number | null` → `teamAverage: number | null` + `teamCount: number`. `loadVendors()` runs the existing vendors + project_vendors SELECTs plus a parallel `from("vendor_ratings").select("vendor_id, rating")` via Promise.all (extra round-trip off the critical path). Client-side aggregate: build a `Map<vendor_id, {sum, count}>` from the ratings result, compute `teamAverage = sum / count` (null when count = 0), merge into the row mapping. Chose spec § 2 Option C (separate query + client merge) over PostgREST inline aggregate embed or a Postgres view — known to work, no PostgREST version dependency, perf cost minimal. **§6.G StarRating component (half-star + md size).** `src/components/data/StarRating.tsx` — size map extended `Record<"sm" | "md" | "lg", number> = { sm: 14, md: 18, lg: 22 }`; `size` prop type widened from `"sm" | "lg"` to `"sm" | "md" | "lg"` (additive, no other call sites affected). Read-only path now supports fractional `value`: per-star branch is `value >= i+1` → fully filled, `value > i` (and `< i+1`) → new `<HalfStar />` overlay (two stacked stars: off-star background + filled-star overlay clipped to left half via `position: absolute; width: px/2; overflow: hidden`), else off-star. Editable path unchanged (still integer-only; hover preview + click both emit whole numbers). Existing integer call sites (`<StarRating value={5} />` etc.) render identically since the new logic collapses to the same shape when `value` is whole. **Type regeneration.** `supabase gen types typescript --linked` after the push surfaces `vendor_ratings: { Row | Insert | Update | Relationships }` and drops `internal_rating` from the vendors Row/Insert/Update column maps. **Build state.** `npx tsc --noEmit` clean after types regen. `npx eslint` clean on the six changed source files (`StarRating.tsx` / `VendorsGlanceEmbed.tsx` / `queries.ts` / `VendorDetail.tsx` / `VendorEdit.tsx` / `VendorsList.tsx`). **Locked decisions (2026-05-18).** (1) Pre-migration count skipped per Jimmie's choice; any vendor with NULL `created_by` lost its legacy rating silently in the backfill. **Predecessor phase:** Phase 5.7.12 (Profile + Profile Settings split surfaces + 5.7.2 @-mention demotion reverts). Twelfth sub-phase of Phase 5.7. One migration (`20260528100000_phase_5_7_12_self_profile_update.sql` — `CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.users_protect_admin_columns()` extended to gate self-writes on `is_owner`, `email`, `full_name` alongside the existing `permission_role` + `active` guards; non-admin updates to any of those columns now raise `Only admins can change <column>` and reject the UPDATE). **Spec deviation §5 (locked 2026-05-18 with Jimmie via "Extend the trigger" option).** Spec § 5 proposed a new `users_update_self` policy + an additive column-list `GRANT UPDATE` to scope the writable set. Both are no-ops against the live schema: `users_update` already permits self-writes via `USING (id = auth.uid() OR public.is_admin())`, and `authenticated` already holds `GRANT SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE ON public.users` (whole-table) from the original `grant_data_api_access.sql` migration — additive column-list grants don't restrict in Postgres. The real gap was the existing `users_protect_admin_columns` trigger which only guarded `permission_role` + `active`, leaving `is_owner`, `email`, `full_name`, `avatar_url` open to self-writes. Picked the trigger extension because it matches the spec's intent ("tier columns stay admin-only") without breaking admin paths and without the REVOKE-and-re-GRANT-everything dance. `avatar_url` deliberately NOT added to the trigger — `useAuth` re-stamps `users.avatar_url` from Google OAuth metadata on every session resolve (one-shot per provider lifecycle, gated by a localStorage flag) and that path runs under the user's own JWT; gating `avatar_url` here would break every non-admin sign-in. Photo-upload escalation surface is narrow (deface own profile photo via devtools, no impact on others). When 5.7.14 lands real photo upload, gating moves to a storage policy on the avatars bucket. **§3 + §6.A new read-only Profile route.** `src/pages/users/UserProfile.tsx` (~225 LoC). Route `/users/:id` registered in `src/App.tsx` between `/users/:id/edit` and the `/team` redirect block so React Router specificity keeps `/users/new` + `/users/:id/edit` winning. Wrapped in the shared `<ProtectedRoute><AppShell />` group (no explicit `<ProtectedRoute>` needed inline; inherited from the parent route at App.tsx line 105). Tier gate handled INSIDE the component, not at the router: `useUserRole().isAdmin` chooses whether the top-right action button reads "Manage user →" (admin path to `/users/:id/edit`) or "Edit your profile →" (self path to `/settings/profile`), and back-link target switches to `/` for Standard + Freelance since `/users` (TeamList) is admin-gated per `<AdminRoute>`. Single SELECT against `users` with `department:departments!users_department_id_fkey(id, name)` embed (constraint-named per `feedback_postgrest_embed_constraint_named_fk.md`). `<LoadError title="User not found" />` on `.maybeSingle()` returning null. Three-card stack below the header: Role & Team (role, department, tier pill via existing TeamList palette, Owner badge if `is_owner`); Contact (email as `mailto:` link with the `inline-block max-w-full truncate align-bottom` brand-rule classes per § 12; Slack "Connected"/"Not connected" via `IconSlack`; @handle); Status (active pill green/grey from existing TeamList pattern, `formatLastActive(last_active_at)` from `src/lib/team/relativeActive.ts`, "Member since {Month YYYY}" derived locally from `created_at`). Avatar rendered as 40px inline `<img referrerPolicy="no-referrer">` with initials fallback (no `UserAvatar` primitive exists; inlined to avoid bikeshedding a new shared component). No InternalNotesEditor on the profile (parent_type union doesn't include `'user'`); no Activity card (carry-forward). **§3 + §6.B new self-only Profile Settings route.** `src/pages/users/ProfileSettings.tsx` (~290 LoC). Route `/settings/profile` registered immediately after `/users/:id` in App.tsx. Loads the viewer's OWN row via `useAuth().user.id`. Form lifts the TeamMemberEdit pattern: `initial` + `form` paired state, `JSON.stringify` dirty check, StickySaveBar visible only when dirty, AlertDialog confirm on Cancel with dirty state. Card stack: Identity (80px avatar inline with "Your avatar comes from your Google account" caption; full_name + email rendered as `<input disabled>` with explainer captions — "Ask an admin to change your name" / "Your sign-in identity. Contact an admin to change."); Role & Team (`<input>` for role_title, `<RecordCombobox source={{kind:"lookup",table:"departments"}}>` for department); Slack (`<input>` for handle with leading-`@` stripped on save via `replace(/^@+/, "")`, `<input>` for user ID with the canonical "Slack → avatar → Profile → More → Copy member ID" caption, link out to `/notifications/preferences` at the bottom of the card). Save UPDATE writes only `role_title`, `department_id`, `slack_handle`, `slack_user_id`. Toast `"Profile updated."` on success (default variant), destructive variant with the Postgres error message on failure. `paddingBottom: 120` per `project_savebar_fixed_position_v3.md`. Missing-row error state renders "We can't find your profile / Contact an admin to get your account linked." for the rare race where `handle_new_user` hasn't fired yet. **§ 2 + §11 demotion reverts (4 sites + 1 mention-href fix).** The 5.7.2 work demoted @-mention spans + activity-feed actor names + record-href targets for non-admin viewers because `/users` (TeamList) was admin-gated and there was no `/users/:id` profile to fall back to. With UserProfile now available to every tier, all four demotions come out: (1) `src/components/data/InternalNotesEditor.tsx` line 385-405 — mention render walk drops the `isAdmin` ternary and always renders `<Link to={`/users/${m.mentioned_user_id}`}>` with coral foreground (coral-reserved-for-hyperlinks brand rule preserved). `isAdmin` state stays because `canDelete` at L424 still uses it. Pre-5.7.2 rows without `mentioned_user_id` fall back to `recordHref: null` (bold-only render, same as the existing `recordIsBoldOnly` branch). **Smoke-test gate.** Build state: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean, `npx eslint` clean on the seven changed files (`UserProfile.tsx` / `ProfileSettings.tsx` / `App.tsx` / `InternalNotesEditor.tsx` / `ActivityFeed.tsx` / `RecentActivityCard.tsx` / `formatSentence.ts`). Vite dev server boots clean (after a one-time `npm install` to pull `@tiptap/extension-image@^3.23.4` into the worktree's node_modules — that dep was added in 5.7.10 but worktree node_modules hadn't been refreshed). Both new routes resolve through `<ProtectedRoute>` to the Google SSO sign-in screen without router errors or runtime exceptions. Full interactive smoke (admin viewing other admin, Standard viewing self, /settings/profile dirty-save round-trip, devtools column-gate rejection) gated by the Google SSO auth wall in claude-preview and deferred to Jimmie's post-merge manual pass per the test plan in spec § 11. **Spec test plan deltas.** Spec § 11 "Confirm column gates: in browser devtools, attempt `permission_role` update → Postgres rejects (insufficient privilege on column permission_role)" — actual error message is `"Only admins can change permission_role"` from the trigger RAISE EXCEPTION, not a privilege error, but the rejection still works. Same for `is_owner` (new "Only admins can change owner status"), `email`, `full_name`. `avatar_url` is intentionally NOT rejected (see deviation note above). **Locked decisions (2026-05-18).** (1) Trigger-extension over add-redundant-policy + no-op-GRANT — closes the actual gap (`is_owner` + `email` + `full_name` self-writes), matches spec intent. **Predecessor phase:** Phase 5.7.11 (Vendor Files & Assets URL list + VendorDetail title-width fix + Internal Rating caption removal). Eleventh sub-phase of Phase 5.7. One migration (`20260527100000_phase_5_7_11_vendor_files.sql` — `CREATE TABLE public.vendor_files (id uuid PK default gen_random_uuid(), vendor_id uuid NOT NULL REFERENCES vendors(id) ON DELETE CASCADE, title text NOT NULL, url text NOT NULL, created_by uuid REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL, created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now())`; btree index `vendor_files_vendor_idx (vendor_id, created_at DESC)`; RLS open-authenticated SELECT/INSERT/DELETE — no UPDATE policy per plan §11.D delete + re-add only; GRANT SELECT/INSERT/DELETE to `authenticated` + GRANT ALL to `service_role`). **RLS posture simplified from plan #22's tier gates (above-pending INSERT, author + producer/admin DELETE) to open-authenticated per Jimmie's 2026-05-18 ask** — no other-tier accounts available to test the freelance/author/admin matrix; tier-gated posture revives later if cross-tier access becomes a need. **§11.A new shared component.** `src/components/data/VendorFilesEditor.tsx` mirrors `<InternalNotesEditor>`'s card shape (list of past rows + per-row delete-X + AlertDialog confirm) but extends with an inline-expand +Add pattern: default-collapsed `+ Add a link` tlink → expands to Title input + URL input + Save/Cancel buttons. State managed locally, NOT tied to VendorEdit's StickySaveBar dirty tracking — adding a file commits immediately; Cancel on the form does NOT roll back file adds (matches Status Notes posture on ProjectEdit). **Predecessor phase:** Phase 5.7.10 (SettingsPage Lookup Lists merge + Wiki image upload + Integrations docstring cleanup). Tenth sub-phase of Phase 5.7. Integrations (display-only placeholder for 5.4)` → `5. Integrations (display-only toggles; wiring lands with notification dispatch in a future phase)` and renumbered the card-stack list now that the merged Lookup Lists card collapsed the standalone Project Categories + Cities pair. The user-facing caption (`Integration toggles are display-only in this release...`) was already correct pre-5.7.10; no UI copy change shipped. **§10.A SettingsPage Lookup Lists merge.** `OTHER_LOOKUPS` array extended with `project_categories` + `cities` at the top, so the unified table now holds all six lookups in this order: Project Categories / Cities / Venue Types / Vendor Capabilities / Vendor Categories / Departments. The standalone `<div className="grid g2">` (lines 78-91 pre-5.7.10) that held two dedicated cards for Project Categories + Cities was deleted outright (no hidden code path; the dead cards are gone). The `counts` state already covered all six tables pre-5.7.10, so no state or type changes needed. **§10.B Wiki image upload.** WikiEditor toolbar gains a single `📷` button after the existing `🔗` Link button. Click → OS file picker (accept `image/*`) → browser-side `resizeImage` (canvas-based, 1200px max width, 0.85 JPEG quality, skips resize when already ≤ cap) → `supabase.storage.from("wiki_images").upload()` with `Date.now()-${sanitized-name}` path → `createSignedUrl(path, 365*24*60*60)` (1-year Supabase max) → `editor.chain().focus().setImage({ src: signedUrl }).run()` inserts the image at cursor position. TipTap `Image` extension aliased as `TiptapImage` on import to avoid colliding with the global `Image` constructor used inside `resizeImage()` (`new Image()`). `WikiEditor` gains a new optional `onImageReady?(storagePath)` prop so the parent can track session uploads. New `.wikipage-img, .wikipage img` CSS rule (in `src/index.css` next to the existing `.wikipage.prose` block) caps `max-width: 100%` + auto height + `var(--radius)` rounding + `12px 0` margin + `display: block` so embedded images respect the editor / read content box on both edit-mode + read-mode renders. **§10.B image cleanup (diff-on-save).** WikiPageEdit grows a `sessionUploads = useRef(makeSessionUploadTracker()).current` that the editor pushes each successful upload path into. On successful save (both create + edit branches) the tracker clears; the edit branch additionally calls `cleanupRemovedWikiImages(initial.body, form.body)` which `storage.remove([...])`s any image paths that left the HTML body. On `onDelete` the page-delete handler extracts every image path from `form.body` via `extractWikiImagePaths` and removes them from storage, then `await sessionUploads.cleanupAll()` flushes any session-uploaded files that might have been added since the last save. The Discard-leave confirm action also awaits `sessionUploads.cleanupAll()` before navigating; an unmount `useEffect` returns a teardown that fires `cleanupAll()` as a safety net for hard route changes that bypass the dialog. Tradeoff (locked 2026-05-18): a browser refresh mid-edit can't reliably await async storage deletes from `beforeunload`, so a small orphan-window exists; carry-forward is a nightly job that diffs `storage.objects` against `extractWikiImagePaths()` over all `wiki_pages.body` rows. **Bucket + RLS posture (locked 2026-05-18, reverses the spec drafter's "public bucket" first instinct).** PRIVATE bucket. SELECT allowed for any `authenticated` user (so signed URLs work for every wiki reader tier including Standard + Freelance). INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE gated on `public.is_admin()` (mirrors `wiki_pages` table RLS exactly, since `<AdminRoute>` already gates the editor route anyway). Embedded `<img src>` URLs in `wiki_pages.body` HTML are 1-year signed URLs; after 1 year unedited pages render broken images until the page is re-edited (acceptable v1 tradeoff; carry-forward is the render-time URL-swap pattern if it bites). **Locked decisions (2026-05-18).** (1) Private bucket + 1-year signed URLs over public bucket (consistency with `wiki_pages` table RLS posture). (2) 1200px canvas resize cap (typical wiki photo / diagram doesn't need more; ~200KB end size for a 4K original). (3) Diff-on-save storage cleanup over an orphan-sweep cron (`cleanupRemovedWikiImages` + page-delete sweep + session-tracker flush covers 99% of the surface; one tiny edge case via beforeunload is the deferred carry-forward). (4) `TiptapImage` import alias over aliasing the global `Image` constructor inside `resizeImage` (cleaner; one-line documented at the import). (5) Unified Lookup Lists card with all six entries; the standalone Project Categories + Cities pair is fully removed (not hidden behind a code path). **Smoke followup (post-implementation, 2026-05-18).** Two visual asks folded into the same squash per one-commit-per-ship. (2) **Integrations card collapsed to a header-only stub.** Dropped the three `<IntegrationRow>` children, the disabled toggles, the per-row dividers, the page-local `IntegrationRow` component, and the trailing `<p className="cap">` caption — the card now renders just `<div className="card-headbar"><span className="h-card">Integrations</span><span className="muted">— Coming Soon</span></div>` with no body and no expand affordance. Integrations`) since the standalone Project Categories + Cities grid is gone. **Carry-forwards.** (1) Orphan wiki-images sweep job (nightly diff of `storage.objects` against `extractWikiImagePaths()` over `wiki_pages.body`) if the `beforeunload`-can't-await-async cleanup gap surfaces real orphans during prod use. Predecessor on `main`: `aab31b9` (Phase 5.7.4 squash). **What the spec said (`OUTPUTS/phase-5-7-5-spec.md` § 5, five sub-items + locked decisions #8 / #9).** § 5.A default-view swap — `/deliverables` flips from calendar to board; new `/deliverables/calendar` route picks up the bare calendar; SURFACE_ROUTES rewires; description copy updated. § 5.B board card + column header reshape — `<BoardColumn<T>>` gains an optional `labelExtra?: ReactNode` prop (added between dot + count via a flex-column wrapper inside `.bcol-head`, so existing tasks board stays untouched); `DeliverablesByProjectBoard` puts the client name (coral link to `/clients/:id`) under the project name in the column header, and rewrites the card body to title + due-date top row + a single `deliverableDueLabel` line ("Due In 9 Days", "Due Today", "Completed 4 Days Ago", etc.). § 5.C list view group-by-project — restructured to render one `<DataTable>` per project group with a section header (project link + coral client link + count) above each; columns become Title / Type / Due (centered two-up cell: relative label left + actual date right) / Status; Project + Assignees columns dropped. Sort is per-group internal (controlled `filterState.sort` binding dropped on this view — locked decision, saved-view sort persistence intentionally doesn't apply here). § 5.D auto-task lifecycle — new `src/lib/deliverables/assigneeSync.ts` diffs prev vs next assignee arrays and INSERTs/DELETEs auto-tasks per added/removed user (title format `"{Client} {Project} {DeliverableTitle} Due"`, due_date inherited, status="To Do", priority="Normal"); 23505 unique-violation swallowed as benign race-retry; both DeliverableDetail's inline `saveAssigneeIds` and DeliverableEdit's `onSave` (create + edit flows) call the helper; `originalAssignedUserIdsRef` snapshots the load value for the edit-flow diff; widened SELECTs on DeliverableDetail + DeliverableEdit + `loadDeliverables` to pull `project → client(id, name)` so the helper resolves the title client-side. § 5.E helper additions — `deliverableDueLabel({dueDate, status, completedAt})` in `src/lib/hq/dates.ts` (title-cased; sibling to existing lowercase `relativeDay`, which keeps its 5+ existing consumers untouched). **Locked decisions confirmed (2026-05-17).** (1) Auto-task `task_assigned` notification ships as-is via the existing `trg_notifications_dispatch_tasks` trigger — informative, the auto-task IS a task assigned to the user; no suppression logic. (2) List view uses internal per-group sort; saved-view sort persistence intentionally doesn't apply to the grouped view (regression by design). (3) Due-split renders as a single two-up cell with `align: "c"` header; no colspan DataTable extension. (4) Auto-task lifecycle helper lives at `src/lib/deliverables/assigneeSync.ts` (app-side over Postgres trigger; only writers are DeliverableDetail + DeliverableEdit, both go through the supabase client; easier to debug, no SECURITY DEFINER surface). **Spec deviations.** `DeliverableDetail.saveField` generic narrowed to `Exclude<keyof DbDeliverable, "project" | "project_id">` to keep the project/project_id keys out of the `[field as string]` Update inference (those have their own dedicated savers). `DeliverableDetail.saveProjectId` sets `row.project.client = null` after a project change because the lean `projectOptions` (`{id, label}`) don't carry the client; auto-task title falls back to `"(no client)"` until a refresh re-runs the join (acceptable per spec § 5.A interaction notes). **Smoke followup round 3 (folded into the same squash).** (1) DataTable merged-header tier collapsed from two rows to one. The round-2 implementation rendered the merged "Due" cell in a top tier with an empty sub-header row below (Title + Status got their labels in the bottom row), producing a visible empty strip under the "Due" label with vertical dividers showing through. Fix: walk columns left-to-right and bucket each ungrouped column as its own single-cell run + each maximal sequence of consecutive same-group columns as a colspanned run; render a single thead row where the merged group cell sits inline alongside the ungrouped headers. Sort affordance on the group cell uses the first grouped column's sort fn. (2) Deliverables FilterBar gains a "Client" chip (`{ key: "clientName", label: "Client", type: "text" }`). The flat row mapping in DeliverablesList already exposes `clientName` so no further plumbing was needed; the existing substring matcher picks it up. (3) `.btn-quickadd` restyled per Jimmie: 24x24px rounded square (6px corner radius), solid coral fill (`hsl(var(--primary))`), bold white IconPlus glyph (strokeWidth 4.5 via inline override). Hover state shifts to `--primary-hover`. **Smoke followup round 2 (folded into the same squash).** (1) Auto-task title simplified per Jimmie: drop the client prefix, render `{ProjectTitle} {DeliverableTitle} Due`. `DeliverableContext.clientName` removed from the helper; ctx callsites in DeliverableDetail + DeliverableEdit drop the lookup. (2) `deliverables.type` retired from the UI as a tracked data point. Title is the only descriptor now. Column removed from queries.ts `DeliverableListRow` + `loadDeliverables` SELECT. DeliverableDetail SELECT + `DbDeliverable` type drop `type`; the inline-edit row removed. DeliverableEdit `FormState` + `EMPTY` + load mapper + insert/update payload + the Type `<Field>` block all drop `type`. FILTER_FIELDS on DeliverablesList drops the Type filter. List view drops the Type column. `deliverables.type` column stays on disk (legacy data preserved; no destructive migration). (3) DataTable extended: optional `group?: string` field on `Column<T>`. When at least one column declares a group, the table renders a TOP-tier header row that walks the columns left-to-right and renders one colspanned `<th>` per run of consecutive same-group columns. Used by the Deliverables grouped list to render a merged "Due" header over two adjacent subcolumns (relative label + actual date). Tasks board / Projects list / etc. don't pass `group` so they stay one-tier. (4) "Due" column split per Jimmie: the single two-up cell becomes two columns (`due_relative` width 160 + `due_date` width 110) under the merged "Due" group header. For Complete and Skipped deliverables the relative cell renders `-` per spec. (5) List subgroup header drops the "X deliverables" count caption; coral round `+` quick-add button takes its place at the right (`.btn-quickadd` CSS class added + safelisted). (6) Inline quick-add mechanic: click `+` prepends a draft row to that group's DataTable with an autofocus title input (placeholder "Venues Deck, Design R1 Deck...") plus `-` placeholders in the Due subcells and a muted "Upcoming" in the Status cell. Enter or blur-with-value INSERTs `{title, project_id, status: 'Upcoming', created_by}`. Escape or blur-empty cancels. On success the Realtime INSERT handler + an explicit `loadDeliverables` refetch surface the new row. **Smoke followup round 1 (folded into the same squash).** Round-1 punch list from Jimmie after first smoke: (1) Deliverable status `In Progress` dropped from the enum + UI; Upcoming covers all future. Backfill migration moves existing `In Progress` rows to `Upcoming`. (2) Auto-task lifecycle hardening: DELETE switched to a single `IN (...)` round-trip with `.select("id")` so the helper returns the actual deleted-row count + console-warns when the match count is less than expected; saveAssigneeIds reordered to run the auto-task sync AFTER the deliverables UPDATE so a failed UPDATE doesn't leave stale auto-task state. (3) `tasks.source_deliverable_id` FK flipped from SET NULL to CASCADE so a deliverable hard-delete takes its surviving auto-tasks with it (walking back the original "manual edits preserved" posture per Jimmie's instruction). (4) `deliverableDueLabel` now appends "on {Weekday}" for any future-due day past tomorrow ("Due In 9 Days on Tuesday"); past-due + today/tomorrow keep their shorter forms. (5) Board card background color scale: complete -> muted green, skipped -> muted grey, upcoming + due ≤7d -> coral, ≤14d -> amber, >14d (or null due) -> grey. Driven by a new `cardClassName` prop on `<BoardView>` + five new safelisted bg classes in `src/index.css`. (6) Board column header text bumped: project title 12px (inline override only when `labelExtra` is present so the tasks board stays untouched), client labelExtra 11.5px. (7) List subgroup header reshape: client name moves to the front (coral link, 11.5px), project name moves second (white bold link, 14px, `color: hsl(var(--foreground))` to defeat the `tlink` coral). (8) List subgroup column widths standardized: Title flex, Type 200px, Due 280px, Status 140px — so tables line up column-to-column across groups. (9) HQ Core edit-page input restyle: new `.hq-form` wrapper class scopes a CSS override that strips `.input` outline + `.input--filled` coral left border + adds hover/focus coral-tint background matching `.combobox-trigger`. Applied to all ten HQ Core edit pages (Project / Task / Deliverable / Venue / Vendor / Client / Person / Team / Wiki / Settings). Talent Scout + Venue Scout forms intentionally untouched. (10) DeliverableEdit Title placeholder ("Venues Deck, Design R1 Deck..."). **Build state.** `npx tsc --noEmit -p tsconfig.app.json` reports 14 pre-existing errors in unrelated files (Build & Tooling #1, baseline confirmed via `git stash` round-trip — no regression from 5.7.5 or its follow-up). `npm run build` clean. **Carry-forwards.** Notes_log orphans on deliverable hard-delete still untracked (parent_id is polymorphic, no FK; same posture as 5.7.3). Auto-task title doesn't update if the deliverable title/project/client is later renamed — manual edits preserved philosophy means existing auto-tasks stay frozen at the title from creation time. Existing `relativeDay` consumers untouched; if a future surface wants the title-cased label outside Deliverables, lift `deliverableDueLabel` to a generic. Auto-task batch toast surfaces only the first error message on partial failure; if Phase 5.7+ assignee bulk-update lands, swap to a count-based summary. Spec: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-7-5-spec.md`.

**Predecessor phase:** **Phase 5.6.5.1 owner delegation + sort persistence propagation + Team page account-link fixes shipped 2026-05-17.** Two 5.6.5 carry-forwards bundled in one squash, plus four follow-on bug fixes surfaced during the AWAITING-gate smoke test. Part A: `users.is_owner` becomes delegable. The `users_protect_admin_columns` trigger gets a new clause via `CREATE OR REPLACE` that requires the caller to be an owner (inline subquery; matches the 5.6.5 RLS pattern, no new SQL function) AND blocks self-revoke. TeamMemberEdit Access card grows an owner-only Owner checkbox (gated on `useUserRole().isOwner`); checkbox is disabled when editing your own row with a caption that surfaces the rule before any save attempt. `is_owner` threads through FormState + SELECT + UPDATE + INSERT. Self-revoke is blocked at both the trigger and the UI, so the last-owner-locks-themselves-out failure mode is structurally impossible without an explicit guardrail. Part B: 5.6.5's sort-persistence pattern (introduced for Projects in `031b53b`) propagates to all six remaining list pages (Tasks / Deliverables / Venues / Vendors / Clients / People). Same 4-line wiring per page; column sort now round-trips through saved views (per-user + global) on every HQ Core list surface. Pattern proven on Projects during 5.6.5 soak. No `docs/schema.md` change (function-body extension, not schema). Spec: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-6-5-1-spec.md`; locked decisions: spec § 14. Carry-forwards: at-least-one-owner safeguard beyond self-revoke (the trigger's self-revoke block makes the locked-out failure mode impossible *as long as* there's at least one owner who can't revoke themselves; an owner can still revoke ANOTHER owner; if delegation chains grow, add an explicit `COUNT(*) >= 1` guard in the trigger); activity logging for owner changes (out per § 14.3; if audit becomes a real ask, add a small `users_owner_change_log` table + AFTER UPDATE trigger fired only when `is_owner` changes); TeamList Owner column (out per § 14.4); pre-existing 13 TS errors in unrelated files carry forward from Build & Tooling #1 (TeamMemberEdit insert fixed this phase; the rest stay); hostile-client test from spec § 11 not run (raw `supabase.from('users').update({ is_owner: true })` from a non-owner admin console — trigger guarantees the DB rejects it; worth running once during the next manual QA pass to confirm the toast renders cleanly). - **Phase 5.7.1 global cleanup + RecordCombobox polish + Quick-Add wiring** (`aa128b8`, shipped 2026-05-17): Squash of `claude/phase-5-7-1-global-cleanup` (single feature commit `785a222`). First sub-phase of Phase 5.7 (Smoke Test Pass 2 cleanup). Pure UI sweep — no schema, no migration, no edge function, no types regen. 26 files, +387/-351. Commit deliberately tagged `[skip netlify]`: Jimmie wants the whole 5.7 sequence to deploy once at the end of the phase to save Netlify credits, so every 5.7 sub-phase squashes with `[skip netlify]` until the final sub-phase ships. **§1.A** RecordCombobox grows an optional `quickCreate?: boolean` prop on `CommonProps`. When set AND `inputValue.trim()` is non-empty, the `+ Add` `CommandItem`'s `onSelect` calls `insertOption({ name: typed })` directly, auto-selects the new option (single or multi), clears input, closes popover; falls through to `setMiniOpen(true)` otherwise. Empty-input click is inert (the affordance reads "+ Add" but does nothing — no modal opens — when there's nothing typed). Failure path keeps the combobox open so the user can retry; relies on `createClientInline` / `createVenueInline`'s existing toast for error messaging. Wired on every Client + Venue record-mode picker across HQ: ProjectEdit Client, ProjectDetail inline Client + Venue (multi), PersonDetail inline Client + Venues (multi), EntryPanel detail Client (Outlook). **§1.B** RecordCombobox sweep audit: Code grepped every remaining `<select>` in the codebase against the spec's §6.B audit table; the table matched reality exactly. Audit surfaced one additional record-mode `<select>` not in the spec table — `EntryPanel.tsx:657` (Outlook **new-entry-form** Client picker, parallel to the detail-edit Client at line 344). Posted to Jimmie at the gate with two `AskUserQuestion` prompts; confirmed to flip with `quickCreate`. All 7 callsites then flipped: TaskEdit Project + Assignee (users), PersonEdit Client (quickCreate) + Vendor (no quickCreate — needs Category), DeliverableEdit Project, VenueEdit Exclusive Vendors (record-multi), EntryPanel new-entry Client (quickCreate). Pattern per flip: add a `useCallback`-stable `loadOptions` returning a `useMemo`'d `Option[]` over the existing in-memory state (no extra round trip). PersonEdit added `loadClientOptions` / `loadVendorOptions` alongside the existing `loadVenueOptions`, plus a `handleCreateClient` wrapping `createClientInline`. VenueEdit collapsed the custom chip-cluster + add-`<select>` widget (~40 lines) into a single `<RecordCombobox multi>` — chips, removal, and add picker all subsumed by combobox built-in multi; removed the now-unused `IconX` import. Exclusions confirmed (enum / UI primitives, no flip): TaskEdit Status + Priority, ProjectEdit Status, DeliverableEdit Status, TeamMemberEdit Tier, WikiPageEdit Visibility, EntryPanel Month/Week/Confidence selects, FilterBar / MiniCreateModal / MultiTagInput / InlineAddSelect primitives. **§1.C** Quick-Add cluster rewrite (`src/components/home/QuickAddCluster.tsx`): 69 → 33 lines. Dropped `useState` + `AlertDialog` + the "Coming in Phase 5.2" stub. `ITEMS` now `[{ label, to }]` pairs; each chip calls `navigate(item.to)` to `/projects|tasks|deliverables|people/new`. Visual treatment (dashed `.hq-qa` + IconPlus) unchanged. **§1.D** Filter / saved-view button order across 8 list pages: filter-side controls left, SavedViewsDropdown right. Projects + Tasks + Deliverables lists: ViewSwitch left, SavedViews right, dead `Columns` + `Save view` placeholder cluster dropped entirely; FilterBar full-width below (unchanged). People list: FilterBar + Affiliation buttons left, SavedViews right (affiliation pill colors per 5.6.2 lock preserved). Clients + Vendors + Venues lists: FilterBar left, SavedViews right. Team list: kept the disabled List `viewswitch` placeholder per spec (5.7.4.E carry-forward), restructured the outer flex from `row between` to `row-c wrap` so viewswitch + FilterBar both sit in a single left cluster. **§1.E** RecentActivityCard cross-team title (`src/components/home/RecentActivityCard.tsx:155`) flips `"Cross-team Activity"` → `"Global Activity Feed"`. Standard scope still `"Recent Activity"`. **§1.F** Google avatar bugfix (both layers shipped). **Layer 1** (chrome rendering): AppShell derives `avatarUrl` from `user.user_metadata.avatar_url`, threads to both `<LeftRail>` (which threads to `<RailFooter>`) + `<TopBar>`. Both shell components accept a new optional `avatarUrl?: string | null` prop; when set, render `<img src={avatarUrl} alt={initials} referrerPolicy="no-referrer" />` inside the existing avatar container; fall back to text initials when null. `referrerPolicy="no-referrer"` is the critical bit — Google's `lh3.googleusercontent.com` 403s on cross-origin `Referer`; the attribute strips the header so the image loads. CSS: `.hq-avatar` + `.hq-rail-av` get `overflow-hidden`; new `.hq-avatar img, .hq-rail-av img` rules set width/height 100%, `object-fit: cover`, `border-radius: inherit`, `display: block`. **Layer 2** (storage stamp): parallel useEffect in `useAuth.tsx` mirrors the 5.6.5.1 `last_active_at` throttle. New `stampedAvatarUserIdRef` useRef (one-shot per provider lifecycle per user.id). On session resolve with a metadata avatar URL: reads sessionStorage key `avatar_url_stamped:${uid}`; if within 5 min, skip. Otherwise SELECTs `users.avatar_url` for the uid, compares with metadata URL; only UPDATEs on diff. SessionStorage stamp written on both paths (success and already-current) so the SELECT doesn't re-fire on every reload. try/catch around all sessionStorage; console.warn on read or write errors; the SELECT/UPDATE wrapped in a self-invoking async IIFE so the effect doesn't return a Promise. Backfills `public.users.avatar_url` for existing users whose auth row predates the metadata capture in `handle_new_user`. **§1.G** Dead-UI strips: TopBar + RailFooter both lose the disabled `Profile (5.4)` `DropdownMenuItem` + the `<DropdownMenuSeparator />` above the sole remaining `Sign out` item + the now-unused `DropdownMenuSeparator` import. ProjectDetail loses the dashed `"No attachments yet"` section (lines 807-812 pre-strip); Tasks section becomes the main column's final child with no layout adjustment needed (intrinsic gap rules hold). ClientDetail loses the `"Files & Assets"` card (lines 449-459 pre-strip); `<InternalNotesEditor>` becomes the main column's final child; now-unused `IconPlus` import removed. VendorDetail's F&A card untouched per spec — 5.7.10 replaces it with the URL list. **Spec deviations flagged**: (1) ProjectEdit Venue picker (§6.A spec inventory) doesn't actually exist on ProjectEdit — Venue lives on ProjectDetail only; skipped silently. (2) VenueEdit Exclusive Vendors collapsed the entire custom chip cluster into one `<RecordCombobox multi>` rather than wrapping only the inner `<select>` (spec implied the latter); cleaner end state, slightly larger diff. (3) PersonEdit Vendor picker flipped without `quickCreate` AND without `miniCreateFields`/`onMiniCreate` either — no `createVendorInline` helper exists in the codebase, so the picker has no `+ Add` affordance (mirrors pre-flip `<select>` behavior; a future phase adds `createVendorInline` + Category-context flow if Vendor inline-create is desired here). **Carry-forwards**: TeamList disabled List `viewswitch` placeholder stays (5.7.4.E owns removal); VendorDetail F&A card stays (5.7.10 owns the URL list rewrite); MultiTagInput primitive `<select>` out of scope; `createVendorInline` helper not yet built (future sub-phase if Vendor pickers need quickCreate). Build: `tsc --noEmit` clean (zero errors — drops the 13 pre-existing TS errors noted in the spec's § 11; either the regen state cleared on a prior commit or the new RecordCombobox flips happened to clear the consumer-side error path); `npm run build` clean (~2.1s, 2025 modules transformed). No schema change, no migration, no types regen, no edge function deploys. Spec slot: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-7-1-spec.md`; phase plan: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-7-plan.md`. Predecessor `d36b516` (Throttle last_active_at stamping to a 5-min floor per user). Single-commit micro-phase from `claude/last-active-throttle` retiring the carry-forward flagged in the 5.6.5.1 SHIPPED block. The 5.6.5.1 effect in `AuthProvider` stamps `users.last_active_at` on every session resolve guarded by a `useRef` (one write per provider lifecycle per user.id) — fine at 5-user scale but tabs in/out + soft remounts could rack up writes if user count grows. Adds a second guard: sessionStorage key `last_active_stamped:${userId}` storing the epoch ms of the last successful stamp; if the stored value is within 5 minutes of `Date.now()`, the effect skips the UPDATE entirely. sessionStorage reads/writes wrapped in `try/catch` for private-mode browsers; on throw the fallback is the existing one-shot-per-lifecycle behavior. Only the success path writes the new timestamp so a failed UPDATE doesn't lock out future retries. No schema change, no migration, no types regen, no edge function deploys. No spec file (micro-phase). Predecessor `b51d62a` (Phase 5.6.5.1: owner delegation + sort persistence propagation + Team page account-link fixes). Squash of `claude/phase-5-6-5-1-owner-delegation` (five feature commits collapsed at the gate: `3476336` main 5.6.5.1 implementation + four follow-on bug fixes surfaced during AWAITING-gate smoke testing — `9d15656` user-create id NULL violation, `9c51c00` Account Status "Linked" false positive, `06dd159` last_active_at stamp on auth resolve, `5a146f1` TeamList accountPill keys on last_active_at). Two 5.6.5 carry-forwards bundled here: (A) owner delegation surface + (B) sort persistence propagation to the remaining 6 list pages. **Part A** extends `users_protect_admin_columns` trigger with an `is_owner` clause via `CREATE OR REPLACE` (no DROP, same OID, same SECURITY DEFINER posture). The new clause fires when `OLD.is_owner IS DISTINCT FROM NEW.is_owner`: require the caller to be an owner via inline `EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM users WHERE id = auth.uid() AND is_owner = true)`, AND block self-revoke (`NEW.id = auth.uid() AND OLD.is_owner = true AND NEW.is_owner = false` raises `Owners cannot revoke their own owner status`). Inline-SELECT shape mirrors the 5.6.5 RLS pattern; avoids introducing a new SQL function surface. TeamMemberEdit Access card grows an Owner checkbox below the existing Tier + Account Status `g2`, owner-only via `useUserRole().isOwner`, with the checkbox disabled when an owner is editing their own row + a caption that swaps to "Another owner must revoke yours." `is_owner` threads through FormState + EMPTY + the SELECT + the shared `payload` used by both edit-UPDATE and create-INSERT paths. Self-revoke is blocked at the trigger AND surfaced in the UI as a disabled checkbox so the rule is visible before any save attempt; structurally kills the last-owner-locks-themselves-out failure mode without an explicit "at least one owner" guardrail. **Part B** propagates the 5.6.5 follow-on (`031b53b`) sort-persistence wiring from ProjectsList to all six remaining list pages (Tasks / Deliverables / Venues / Vendors / Clients / People). Same 4-line addition per page: `sort={filterState.sort ?? null}` + `onSortChange={(next) => setFilterState((prev) => ({ ...prev, sort: next }))}`. Pattern proven on Projects during 5.6.5 soak. Column sort now round-trips through saved views (per-user + global) on every HQ Core list surface. **Follow-on bug fixes absorbed in the same squash, all surfaced during AWAITING-gate smoke testing:** (1) User-create id NULL violation. TeamMemberEdit's create-flow insert omitted `users.id` (NOT NULL, no DB default — Phase 5.4 dropped the FK to auth.users(id) for the id-swap pattern). Fix: pass `id: crypto.randomUUID()` in the insert payload. Clears the pre-existing TS error at TeamMemberEdit.tsx:164 (one of the 14 in Build & Tooling #1; 13 remain). (2) Account Status "Linked" false positive on the edit page. `accountLinked` derived from `permission_role !== 'pending'`, but the create form defaults new users to `'standard'` and `TIER_OPTIONS` omits `'pending'` entirely, so every pre-provisioned user falsely showed as Linked. Fix: derive from `last_active_at !== null` — `handle_new_user` stamps it on auth.users INSERT, so it's the authoritative signal. (3) `last_active_at` never updated post-signup. `handle_new_user` only fires on auth.users INSERT; subsequent sign-ins don't re-stamp, so users whose auth row predates the column add (Jimmie, Ali) stayed NULL and read as Pending after fix #2. Fix: add a one-shot effect in `AuthProvider` that updates `last_active_at` when `session.user.id` resolves. Guarded by a `useRef` so it fires once per provider lifecycle per user.id; RLS allows self-update via `users_update`, and `last_active_at` isn't gated by the protect trigger. Existing seeded users self-backfill on their next page load — no backfill migration needed. (4) TeamList accountPill same false positive. Switched the pill's signature from `(role: PermissionRole)` to `(lastActiveAt: string | null)` and keyed on nullability. AdminsCard uses `permission_role` only for admin/non-admin filtering (correct usage) — no fix needed there. One migration applied at the squash gate (function body change only): `20260521100000_phase_5_6_5_1_owner_column_gate.sql`. No types regen needed (trigger function bodies don't surface in generated TS); ran as sanity check + produced no diff. No edge function deploys. No `docs/schema.md` change (the column gate is a function-body extension, not a schema change). Spec: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-6-5-1-spec.md`; locked decisions: spec § 14. Predecessor `069895d` (Phase 5.6.5: global default views (owner admin)). Squash of `claude/ecstatic-keller-4f211e` (two feature commits collapsed at the gate: `13a2553` main 5.6.5 implementation + `031b53b` sort-persistence follow-on for Projects). Owner-admin feature giving Jimmie (and any future delegated owner) a way to publish a default view that every user sees on mount across all seven HQ Core list pages + the unified Calendar. Standard / freelance can still override the global with their own per-user default; resolution is per-user → global → unfiltered. Net-new behavior: `getDefaultSavedView` has existed since 5.2.1 but was never called from any page — this is the first phase that wires it across all list surfaces. New `users.is_owner` boolean column (NOT NULL DEFAULT false; backfilled `true` for `email='jimmie@mirrornyc.com'`); new `saved_views.scope` text column (NOT NULL DEFAULT `'user'`, CHECK in `'user' / 'global'`); `saved_views.entity_type` CHECK widened to include `'vendor'` + `'client'` (the list pages have been passing these since 5.2.3 but the CHECK rejected them silently; zero rows in production today so no backfill risk; `'organization'` stays in the CHECK as a back-compat legacy value); new partial index `saved_views_scope_default_idx ON (scope, entity_type) WHERE scope = 'global' AND is_default = true` speeds up the global-default lookup that fires on every list-page mount. All four `saved_views` RLS policies replaced with scope-aware versions: SELECT allows `user_id = auth.uid() OR scope = 'global'`; INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE branched on scope (`scope='user'` requires `user_id = auth.uid()`; `scope='global'` requires `(SELECT is_owner FROM public.users WHERE id = auth.uid()) = true` — inline subquery matches the `is_admin()` shape; no new SQL function). `useUserRole` gains `isOwner: boolean` derived from a new `is_owner` field in the users SELECT. `src/lib/hq/savedViews.ts`: `EntityType` widened to add `'vendor'`, `'client'`, `'calendar'` (latter was already in the DB CHECK since 5.3 but missing from the TS type; `'organization'` marked `@deprecated`); `SavedViewScope` exported; `SavedView` gains `scope`; `createSavedView` now requires a `scope` param (forces callers to think); `getDefaultSavedView` rewritten to resolve per-user → global → null; new `resetUserDefault(entityType)` flips the per-user default flag to false without deleting the row; new `hasGlobalDefault(entityType)` returns whether a global default exists. `<SavedViewsDropdown>` gains owner-only "Save as default for all users" checkbox inside the Save dialog (mutually exclusive with "Make this my default view" — the per-user option hides when global is ticked) + new "Reset to global default" item in the dropdown popover, visible only when a per-user default exists for this entity AND a global default exists. New optional `onResetToGlobal` callback prop lets the parent re-resolve and apply immediately (no page reload). The popover row's `default` badge renders `global default` when `scope === 'global'`. `useCalendarVisibility` load logic now does per-user row → global row → first-visit insert with source-aware defaults; when reading from a global row, the next toggle INSERTs a per-user row (which then becomes the source of truth); new `hasPerUserRow` returned flag + new `refresh()` callback re-runs the load effect via a tick counter. `<VisibilityPanel>` accepts new `canPublishGlobal` / `canResetToGlobal` / `onPublishGlobal` / `onResetToGlobal` props; renders the two buttons between the divider and the Projects section header (owner button in primary coral, reset button in plain `.tlink` style). `CalendarPage` owns the handlers: `handlePublishGlobalCalendarDefault` does clear-then-set (clears any prior global `__calendar_default`, inserts a new global row with the current state); `handleResetCalendarToGlobal` DELETEs the user's per-user `__calendar_default` row (flipping `is_default = false` doesn't work because the hook reads any per-user row by name, not by flag), then calls `visibility.refresh()`. All seven list pages (ProjectsList / TasksList / DeliverablesList / VenuesList / VendorsList / ClientsList / PeopleList) get an on-mount `getDefaultSavedView(entityType)` effect + a `handleResetToGlobal` handler wired to the dropdown's new prop. TasksList coordinates the new default-view loader with the existing "My open tasks" baseline via a `savedViewAppliedRef` so the baseline only fires when no saved view loaded. Smoke-test follow-on (`031b53b`, landed as a separate feature commit on the branch and squashed in here): persists sort in saved views, Projects only as a first pass. `FilterState` gains optional `sort?: FilterSort | null` (`FilterSort = { key, dir }`, matches DataTable's internal `SortState` shape). `<DataTable>` becomes optionally-controlled-sort via new `sort` + `onSortChange` props (when both omitted, internal state still wins — the other 6 list pages keep working unchanged). ProjectsList passes `filterState.sort` + the setter to DataTable so column sort round-trips through saved views (per-user + global) automatically since the whole filterState is what `createSavedView` writes and `getDefaultSavedView` restores. Tasks / Deliverables / Venues / Vendors / Clients / People stay on internal-sort behavior; carry-forward to propagate after Projects soaks. One migration applied at the squash gate: `20260520100000_phase_5_6_5_saved_views_global_scope_users_is_owner.sql`. types regen produced the expected delta (`users.is_owner` boolean on Row/Insert/Update; `saved_views.scope` text on Row/Insert/Update) plus cleared a pre-existing `Initialising login role...` stderr leak that had been at the top of `src/integrations/supabase/types.ts` since Phase 5.6.3 (`c29c8bd`); the clean parse exposed 14 pre-existing TS errors in unrelated files (TaskDetail, VendorDetail, VenueDetail, ProjectDetail, ClientDetail, PersonDetail, DeliverableDetail, TeamMemberEdit, SettingsPage, PullDetail, ErrorState, `lookups.ts`, `vendors/queries.ts`) that the corruption had been masking; logged as Build & Tooling #1 in `code-observations.md` and out of scope for 5.6.5 (Vite build still passes; Vite doesn't type-check by default). `docs/schema.md` updated: § users gains the `is_owner` line; § saved_views gains the `scope` line, widens the `entity_type` CHECK list, notes the calendar-shape filter_state variant, mentions the global-scope clear-then-set on `is_default`, replaces the RLS line with the scope-aware posture, and adds the new partial index. Cross-cutting primitive plumbing: `src/lib/hq/lookups.ts` refactored from per-hook React state to a module-level subscriber cache (`Map<key, {options, loading, subscribers}>`) keyed on `${table}:${parentScopeId}` so every mounted `useLookup(table)` instance sees a fresh `addOption` insert immediately. Without this, an inline-add inside a `RecordCombobox` updated only the combobox's own hook state; the parent page's `useLookup` was stale until full refresh, so the parent's `onChange` callback (running in the same tick) couldn't resolve the new name → id and the option failed to auto-select. New `getLookupCached(table, parentScopeId)` sync accessor lets parent `onChange` handlers fall back to a direct cache read when their closure-captured snapshot lags by one render (the cache mutates synchronously inside `addOption` before the subscriber-notify fires). Applied as the no-clobber pattern across VendorDetail Category + Subcategory + every other lookup-driven `onChange` in the sweep. RecordCombobox: single-mode `handlePick` was already toggle-off-on-reclick from 5.6.3; LookupSource type extended with `parentScopeLabel` + `parentScopeLabelKey` (threaded into a new `miniCreateContext` prop on `ComboboxView` then on `MiniCreateModal`). MiniCreateModal: gained a `context?: { label, value }[]` prop that renders read-only kv rows in a tinted bordered card above the editable fields; wired in VendorDetail + VendorEdit subcategory comboboxes so users see "Category: Catering" (or whatever) before naming the new subcategory. Polish round absorbed: `.label-section` 12px → 13px; `.tag` 10.5px → 12px; `.kv` row-gap 11px → 22px and `.kv dt` 11px → 12px so inline-edit fields breathe; `.kv--pair` (10px row-gap helper) added for date-pair tight grouping; `.kv dd` gets `min-width:0` so the 1fr value column can shrink below intrinsic content width on resize (multi-select chip rows on ProjectDetail Venue were spilling out of the card before this); `.inline-edit-read` hover affordance + `.inline-edit-input` coral focus ring CSS pair; `.fchip--btn` / `.fchip--active` toggle filter button styling; PersonDetail Edit button reduced to pencil-only (text removed per Jimmie's review).
