- **`last_active_at` stamping throttled to a 5-min floor per user** (`d36b516`, shipped 2026-05-17): single-commit micro-phase retiring the carry-forward flagged in the 5.6.5.1 SHIPPED block. The 5.6.5.1 effect in `AuthProvider` stamps `users.last_active_at` on every session resolve guarded by a `useRef` (one write per provider lifecycle per user.id) — fine at current 5-user scale but tabs in/out + soft remounts could rack up writes if user count grows. Adds a sessionStorage second guard: key `last_active_stamped:${userId}` storing the epoch ms of the last successful stamp; if the stored value is within 5 minutes of `Date.now()`, the effect skips the UPDATE entirely. Only writes the new timestamp on a successful UPDATE so a failed write doesn't lock out future retries. sessionStorage reads/writes wrapped in `try/catch` — private-mode browsers throw on access; on throw the fallback is the existing one-shot-per-lifecycle behavior. Two-layer guard now: the prior `useRef` (covers React StrictMode double-mount and tab-focus re-renders within a single page load) plus the new sessionStorage check (covers manual reloads + route changes that remount the provider tree, scoped to the 5-min floor per tab). No schema change, no migration, no types regen, no edge function deploys, no doc updates beyond CHECKPOINT.md. Spec: none (single-file micro-phase from the 5.6.5.1 carry-forward).

- **Phase 5.6.5.1 owner delegation + sort persistence propagation + Team page account-link fixes** (`b51d62a`, shipped 2026-05-17): two 5.6.5 carry-forwards bundled in one squash plus four follow-on bug fixes surfaced during the AWAITING-gate smoke test. **Part A — Owner delegation.** `users_protect_admin_columns` trigger gets a new clause via `CREATE OR REPLACE` (no DROP, same OID, no policy-dep audit) that gates `is_owner` writes to owners only via inline `EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM users WHERE id = auth.uid() AND is_owner = true)` — matches the 5.6.5 RLS inline-subquery shape; avoids introducing a new SQL function surface. Same clause blocks self-revoke: `NEW.id = auth.uid() AND OLD.is_owner = true AND NEW.is_owner = false` raises `Owners cannot revoke their own owner status`. TeamMemberEdit Access card grows an Owner checkbox below the existing Tier + Account Status g2, owner-only via `useUserRole().isOwner`; checkbox is disabled when an owner edits their own row + a caption surfaces the rule ("Another owner must revoke yours.") before the user can attempt a save. `is_owner` threads through FormState + the SELECT + the shared `payload` used by both edit-UPDATE and create-INSERT paths. The trigger AND the UI together kill the last-owner-locks-themselves-out failure mode structurally without an explicit "at least one owner" guardrail. **Part B — Sort persistence propagation.** The 5.6.5 follow-on (`031b53b`) lifted DataTable sort to a controlled prop pair (`sort` + `onSortChange`) + added `FilterState.sort?: FilterSort | null`. ProjectsList was wired during 5.6.5; this phase propagates the same 4-line addition (`sort={filterState.sort ?? null}` + `onSortChange={(next) => setFilterState((prev) => ({ ...prev, sort: next }))}`) to all six remaining list pages: Tasks / Deliverables / Venues / Vendors / Clients / People. Column sort now round-trips through saved views (per-user + global) on every HQ Core list surface. Pattern proven on Projects during 5.6.5 soak. **Follow-on bug fixes absorbed in the same squash, all surfaced during AWAITING-gate smoke testing:** (1) user-create id NULL violation. TeamMemberEdit's create-flow insert omitted `users.id` (NOT NULL, no DB default — Phase 5.4 dropped the FK to auth.users(id) for the id-swap pattern); fix passes `id: crypto.randomUUID()` in the insert payload. handle_new_user swaps the placeholder to the auth uid on first sign-in via email match. Clears the pre-existing TS error at TeamMemberEdit.tsx:164 (one of the 14 in Build & Tooling #1; 13 remain). (2) Account Status "Linked" false positive on the edit page. `accountLinked` derived from `permission_role !== 'pending'`, but the create form defaults new users to `'standard'` and `TIER_OPTIONS` omits `'pending'` entirely, so every pre-provisioned user falsely read as Linked. Fix derives from `last_active_at !== null` instead. (3) `last_active_at` never updated post-signup. `handle_new_user` only fires on auth.users INSERT (Phase 5.4); subsequent sign-ins don't re-stamp, so users whose auth row predates the column add (Jimmie, Ali) stayed NULL and read as Pending after fix #2 landed. Fix adds a one-shot effect in `AuthProvider` that updates `last_active_at` when `session.user.id` resolves; guarded by a `useRef` so it fires once per provider lifecycle per user.id; cheap enough at HQ's user count that throttling isn't worth the complexity. RLS allows self-update via the existing `users_update` policy; `last_active_at` isn't gated by the protect trigger. Existing seeded users self-backfill on next page load — no backfill migration needed. (4) TeamList accountPill same false positive. Switched the pill's signature from `(role: PermissionRole)` to `(lastActiveAt: string | null)` and keyed on nullability. AdminsCard uses `permission_role` only for admin/non-admin filtering (correct usage) — no fix needed there. One migration applied (function body change only): `20260521100000_phase_5_6_5_1_owner_column_gate.sql`. No types regen needed (ran as sanity check, no diff). No edge function deploys. No `docs/schema.md` change (function-body extension, not schema). Spec: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-6-5-1-spec.md`; locked decisions: spec § 14. Branch was `claude/phase-5-6-5-1-owner-delegation` (worktree retargeted from `claude/ecstatic-keller-4f211e` at the start of this phase since main had already absorbed the 5.6.5 squash; spec branch name honored this time). Carry-forwards: at-least-one-owner safeguard beyond self-revoke (if delegation chains grow, add an explicit `COUNT(*) >= 1` guard in the trigger); activity logging for owner changes (out per § 14.3; consider a small `users_owner_change_log` table if audit becomes a real ask); TeamList Owner column (out per § 14.4); pre-existing 13 TS errors in unrelated files (was 14 pre-5.6.5.1; TeamMemberEdit insert fixed this phase); hostile-client test from spec § 11 not run during the ship flow.

- **Phase 5.6.5 global default views (owner admin)** (`069895d`, shipped 2026-05-17): owner-admin feature giving Jimmie (and any future delegated owner) a way to publish a default view that every user sees on mount across all seven HQ Core list pages + the unified Calendar. Standard / freelance can still override the global with their own per-user default; resolution is per-user → global → unfiltered. New `users.is_owner` boolean (backfilled `true` for `email='jimmie@mirrornyc.com'`); new `saved_views.scope` (`'user' / 'global'`, NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user'); `saved_views.entity_type` CHECK widened to include `'vendor'` + `'client'` (list pages have been passing these since 5.2.3 but the CHECK silently rejected them; zero rows in production today); new partial index on `(scope, entity_type) WHERE scope='global' AND is_default=true`. Four `saved_views` RLS policies replaced with scope-aware versions: SELECT widens to `user_id = auth.uid() OR scope = 'global'`; INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE branched on scope (`scope='user'` requires `user_id = auth.uid()`; `scope='global'` requires `(SELECT is_owner FROM users WHERE id = auth.uid()) = true` — inline subquery mirrors `is_admin()` shape; no new SQL function so no future drop-dependency risk). `useUserRole` gains `isOwner`. `src/lib/hq/savedViews.ts`: `EntityType` widened (adds `'vendor'`, `'client'`, `'calendar'`; `'organization'` marked `@deprecated`); `SavedView` gains `scope`; `createSavedView` requires a `scope` param; `getDefaultSavedView` rewritten to resolve per-user → global → null; new `resetUserDefault` + `hasGlobalDefault` helpers. Net-new behavior: `getDefaultSavedView` has existed since 5.2.1 but was never called from any page — this is the first phase that wires it across all list surfaces. `<SavedViewsDropdown>` gains owner-only "Save as default for all users" checkbox inside the Save dialog (mutually exclusive with "Make this my default view" — per-user option hides when global is ticked) + "Reset to global default" menu item (visible when a per-user default exists AND a global default exists) wired through new `onResetToGlobal` callback that re-resolves + applies without a page reload. The popover's `default` badge renders `global default` for `scope='global'` rows. `useCalendarVisibility` load logic now does per-user row → global row → first-visit insert; when reading from a global row, the next toggle INSERTs a per-user row (which then becomes the source of truth); new `hasPerUserRow` flag + new `refresh()` callback drive the post-reset reload. `<VisibilityPanel>` accepts new `canPublishGlobal` / `canResetToGlobal` / `onPublishGlobal` / `onResetToGlobal` props; renders the two buttons between the divider and the Projects section header. CalendarPage owns the handlers: `handlePublishGlobalCalendarDefault` does clear-then-set; `handleResetCalendarToGlobal` DELETEs the user's per-user row (the hook reads by name not by `is_default`), then calls `visibility.refresh()`. All seven list pages (Projects / Tasks / Deliverables / Venues / Vendors / Clients / People) get an on-mount `getDefaultSavedView` effect + `handleResetToGlobal` handler. TasksList coordinates the new loader with its existing "My open tasks" baseline via a `savedViewAppliedRef` so the baseline only applies when no saved view loaded. Smoke-test follow-on (`031b53b`, landed as a separate feature commit + squashed in here): sort persistence in saved views, Projects first as a test. `FilterState` gains optional `sort?: FilterSort | null` (`FilterSort = { key, dir }`, matches DataTable's internal `SortState` shape); `<DataTable>` becomes optionally-controlled-sort via new `sort` + `onSortChange` props (when both omitted, internal state still wins so the other 6 list pages keep working unchanged); ProjectsList passes `filterState.sort` + the setter so column sort round-trips through saved views (per-user + global) automatically since the whole filterState is what `createSavedView` writes and `getDefaultSavedView` restores. Smoke test confirmed sort persistence working on Projects (Job # sort retained across navigation + survives global default save). One migration applied at the squash gate: `20260520100000_phase_5_6_5_saved_views_global_scope_users_is_owner.sql`. types regen produced the expected delta (`users.is_owner`; `saved_views.scope`) AND cleared a pre-existing `Initialising login role...` stderr leak that had been at the top of `src/integrations/supabase/types.ts` since Phase 5.6.3 (`c29c8bd`); the clean parse exposed 14 pre-existing TS errors in unrelated files (TaskDetail / VendorDetail / VenueDetail / ProjectDetail / ClientDetail / PersonDetail / DeliverableDetail / TeamMemberEdit / SettingsPage / PullDetail / ErrorState / `lookups.ts` / `vendors/queries.ts`) that the corruption had been masking; logged as Build & Tooling #1 in `code-observations.md` and out of scope for 5.6.5 (Vite build still passes; Vite doesn't type-check by default). `docs/schema.md` updated: § users gains `is_owner`; § saved_views gains `scope` + widened `entity_type` CHECK + new partial index + scope-aware RLS posture. No edge functions, no Realtime additions. Spec: `OUTPUTS/phase-5-6-5-spec.md`; locked decisions: spec § 14. Carry-forwards: propagate sort persistence from Projects to the other 6 list pages (same pattern, ~4 added lines per page; soak Projects first); the 14 TS errors in unrelated files surfaced by the types.ts cleanup (Vite build passes today; recommend a dedicated cleanup pass once Jimmie wants `tsc --noEmit` in CI); no visual screenshot pass at the gate (Jimmie was smoke-testing in the dev server live); spec § 11 permission-tier QA (owner vs admin vs standard vs freelance) requires multiple sign-ins not run yet; `organization` legacy value in saved_views.entity_type CHECK eligible for cleanup migration; owner audit traceability (who set the global) available via `created_by ↔ user_id` link but not surfaced in UI; cross-tab Realtime propagation of global defaults deferred (owner publishes → users see on next page load).

  - Pull pipeline (manual trigger; scheduled pulls land in Phase 3.8). Running-state UI shows a 4-step checklist (search → dedupe → process → save) live-updating via Realtime.
  - **Referral ingestion**: `ts-pull-candidates` detects forwards from `*@mirrornyc.com` to `jobs@mirrornyc.com`, unwraps the chain to find the original applicant. Handles standard Gmail forwards, Apple Mail desktop + mobile (`Begin forwarded message:` and `On <date> <Name> <<email>> wrote:` reply-quote attributions), and forward-as-attachment (`message/rfc822`). Captures any `@mirrornyc.com` manager's commentary along the chain into `ts_candidates.internal_notes` (Mirror signatures stripped) so it factors into the FIRST evaluation via the `HIRING MANAGER NOTES:` block in the candidate bundle. `mirrornyc.com` blocked from portfolio URL extraction so manager signatures don't leak as portfolio links.
  - RoleDashboard with Mirror-grey section cards, master pool table titled in-card ("MASTER POOL · from all rounds"), stat tiles, pull-round cards, two-tier candidate table with bulk actions, "View Final Review" button when one exists.
  - PullDetail: title leads, RX + status (Running / Failed) + Latest pills follow at matched height. Same shared CandidateTable + round-scoped re-eval (parallel fan-out, cancellable).
  - CandidateTable: Resume + Portfolio collapsed into one stacked text-button column (no header text), candidate column 220px, score bar proportional fill on `bg-input` track, status column elements (StatusDropdown + ReviewedPill + ReferralPill) at 12px text. ReferralPill is electric blue (Mirror coral was tried in 3.7.8.8 and reverted in 3.7.8.13 because the brand color blended into too many other coral surfaces).
  - CandidateDetail with header cluster simplified: Re-evaluate button (160px wide, full-height of left column) + right-column stack (auto/manual + referral pills on top, status dropdown on bottom). Tier pill removed (overlapped with status). Score Breakdown with vertical muted-grey tier dividers + tighter criterion rows. Internal Notes editor pre-populated when the candidate is a referral with manager commentary.
  - **Phase 3.6 final review** (`ts-final-review`): comparative AI ranking of the master pool, returns immediately, streams `step_progress` via Realtime, writes `final_rankings` (`{candidate_id, final_rank, final_tier, rationale, recruiter_note}` where `recruiter_note` is `string[]` max 3) to `ts_final_reviews`. FinalReviewDetail page renders the rankings table with rationale + bulleted recruiter note.
  - **Global Settings** (admin only) under `/talent-scout/settings`: global competitor list edit (Postgres `text[]`, seeded with Mirror's 19-entry default), default applicable to all roles unless overridden per-role. Phase 3.8 added Anthropic Monthly Spend Cap input + inline current-spend display (coral $X.XX).
  - All three Talent Scout Claude prompts consolidated in `supabase/functions/_shared/prompts.ts`. Frontend mirror at `src/lib/talent-scout/defaultEvalPrompt.ts` (manually synced; verified byte-for-byte at 3.7.7.6).
  - Toasts site-wide use solid Mirror coral with white text (Sonner + Radix Toast both default to coral).

The wizard step-3 page and Edit Role page both surface a Process / Save button morph: when scorecard has unrefined edits, the action runs the refine pass; once clean, it flips back to Lock (wizard) or Save (Edit Role, which triggers bulk re-eval). Each criterion now carries TWO describer fields: `full_points_rubric` (substantive 1-3 sentences, what the per-candidate evaluator reads) and `summary` (≤ 14-word recap for compact UI surfaces). Both generated in same Claude pass. Existing roles upgrade by re-running scorecard generation OR clicking "Process scorecard" on wizard / Edit Role (Phase 3.10).

## What's NOT live yet

- Cron schedules are committed but require runtime activation: production GUCs (`app.supabase_url` + `app.internal_api_secret`) need to be set in Supabase SQL editor before the schedules will fire. Until then they're scheduled-but-noop.
- All Phase 3.8 edge functions need to be deployed via `supabase functions deploy <name>` (cron functions + `ts-send-pull-notification` + re-deploys for `ts-pull-candidates` and any function that imports `_shared/anthropic.ts`).
- Phase 3.8 migrations need to be pushed: `supabase db push --linked`.
- HQ Core surfaces still stubbed: Activity Feed (5.5), Search (later), Wiki (5.4), Team (5.4), Settings (5.4). Projects + Tasks + Deliverables + Clients + Vendors + People + Venues are all live as of 5.2.3. ~~Calendar (unified, 5.3)~~ + ~~Outlook (5.3)~~ shipped 2026-05-16; per-surface Calendar tabs on Projects + Tasks route to `/calendar?source=projects|tasks` and pre-filter the visibility panel on first visit.
- In-app notifications bell (Phase 5.5). The bell icon ships in 5.1 as visual chrome only; pull-completion email + the new `notify-admin-of-pending-user` admin email are live, but the in-app panel + per-user prefs come later.

## Known issues / drift

- `auto_rejected` enum value is deprecated (Phase 3.7.2.1 backfilled to `reject` + `manually_reviewed=false`) but kept in the enum for safety. New writes never use it. Cleanup requires enum rebuild; not worth it now.
- **Phase 4 Revision deferred items** (not blocking): defense-in-depth sanitization of producer free-text before Claude prompt interpolation in `vs-research-venues` / `vs-generate-brief-overview` (uniform pass, should also cover the pre-existing `brief_data.notes` injection); `vs-generate-brief-overview` (like every VS function) uses the service-role client rather than a caller-JWT client (security-auditor SHOULD-FIX, deferred per spec § 5d "same auth posture" -- harden as a uniform pass); `SCOUT_SELECT` column string duplicated across the three Brief pages. Flagged by security-auditor / code-reviewer and recorded in the squash commit messages.
- **Phase 5.2.3 deferred items** (not blocking): ~~distinct rail icon for Clients (currently shares `IconOrgs` with Vendors)~~ RESOLVED in Phase 5.2 cleanup `65159a2` (new `IconClients` briefcase glyph); ~~`vendors.primary_address` column + VendorEdit field (5.2.3 spec § 4.B.3 visual contract gap; lands in the same polish pass that handles `clients.primary_address` UX uniformity)~~ RESOLVED in Phase 5.2 cleanup `65159a2` (migration `20260516140000` + VendorEdit textarea + VendorDetail kv row); ~~`vendor_capabilities` GRANT lacks DELETE (renamed from org_capabilities; same dead-policy posture; widen alongside Settings page CRUD in 5.4)~~ RESOLVED in Phase 5.2 cleanup `65159a2` (migration `20260516140000` adds the GRANT); VendorDetail "Projects Touched" inefficient client-side filter through `venues.exclusive_vendor_ids` (switch to PostgREST `.contains(...)` push-down when scale warrants, OR add a dedicated `project_vendors` join table if direct project-vendor relationships surface); drop `/organizations/*` backward-compat redirect (`OrganizationsRedirect`) once Mirror bookmarks have updated. Wireframe-v2 redraw of Surface 10 (currently shipped as DEVIATION from the locked wireframe; deferred polish pass).
- **Phase 5.2 cleanup deferred items** (not blocking): `useClientsAndVendors` single-shot load (no cross-tab refresh; observation Frontend #2); `FilterBar.chipDisplayValue` raw-uuid flash race if a saved view restores a lookup chip before lookupOptions has loaded (observation Frontend #3); `docs/schema.md` full 5.2.3 split structural rewrite + new lookup-tables documentation (observation Docs #1; cleanup only added a drift callout + delta bullets for its own changes); ~~§ 4.5 manual-push stale-sync risk if Jimmie aborts at step 5e after the SHIPPED block has already written (observation Docs #2)~~ RESOLVED in `5b14bfe` + the `Bash(git push origin main)` allowlist (`85cb765`); Tags filter `"any-of"` upgrade + `applyFilters` array-vs-array intersection fix (deferred until a real UX driver).
- **Phase 5.3 deferred items** (not blocking): `<CalendarMonthView />` now has two render paths (controlled-vs-uncontrolled; observation Frontend #6); CalendarPage Lead + Category FilterChip popovers do not close on outside click (observation Frontend #5; promote to shadcn `<Popover>` later); `<OutlookEntryPanel />` fires `useClients()` + `useLookup("cities")` queries even in detail mode where neither is used (deferred, admin-only + cheap); `loadDistinctOutlookYears` selects all rows for distinct extraction (deferred, small table); `ProjectDetail` "Days Until Install" stat tile now prefers `install_dates_start` over `live_dates_start` (observation Frontend #7; document for producers so the countdown behavior change isn't surprising for projects with only live dates set); concurrent first-visit `saved_views` race on the Calendar page (two tabs simultaneously on first visit could both attempt the INSERT; second falls back silently to default state; deferred, low impact); `MIRROR_HOLIDAYS` carries only a single Jan 1 2027 stub (cliff in early 2027; extend in 5.4 Settings editor when the 2027 PDF is published); `outlook_entries` not in the `supabase_realtime` publication (single-admin edit pattern; add later if multi-admin concurrent editing surfaces as a need); CalendarMonthView's `outlook_entries` query against the linked DB uses generic-string casts (`as never`) in `src/lib/calendar/queries.ts` because the types weren't yet regenerated when the file was written; post-squash regen now backs them but the casts remain in source.
- **Phase 5.2.2 activity_log_writer fix** (not blocking, applied as `20260516120004`): the shipped trigger function evaluated `OLD.status IS DISTINCT FROM NEW.status` inside an AND expression that doesn't short-circuit RECORD field access. UPDATE on tables without a status column (people, organizations, venues, the new lookups) crashed. Fix: nested-IF guard so OLD.status only resolves for `('projects', 'tasks', 'deliverables')`, plus `to_jsonb()->>'status'` defense-in-depth (returns NULL on missing keys instead of erroring). Pasted into Supabase Studio at the squash-approval gate before the seed; backfilled into the migration ledger via the `_004` file so future fresh checkouts see it as applied DDL.
- **Phase 5.1 deferred items** (not blocking): `notes_log` Realtime publication + `REPLICA IDENTITY FULL` will need to land when 5.2's Notes UI ships if it uses `postgres_changes` subscriptions (migration-reviewer flag); `notes_log` SELECT policy is currently `USING (true)` to authenticated, which includes `pending` users — narrow to `is_standard_or_admin OR is_admin` in 5.4 when the Team page locks tier-access patterns (migration-reviewer flag); server-side `hashAsStringArray` in `vs-generate-brief-overview` does not filter empty-trimmed strings while the client `asStringArray` does, so a direct DB edit injecting `""` into a brief_data array would cause a hash mismatch and one wasted regen (security-auditor flag); existing pages (Talent Scout, Venue Scout) lost the previous `max-w-7xl` shell wrapper and now expand to the full content width inside `.hq-content` (32px padding) — acceptable for 5.1 per spec § 2 "body content untouched"; revisit if any TS / VS surface looks broken at >1440px.
- **Phase 4 Revision pass 3 hash-parity edge case** RESOLVED in Phase 5.1 NIT pickup: `computeOverviewSourceHash` + the server hash now use canonical numeric values for `budget` + `expected_guest_count`, so non-canonical input (no `$` / commas) hashes the same as canonical input. Both sides deployed as v3 of `vs-generate-brief-overview`. `code-observations.md` Frontend #1 closed.

20260531170000_phase_5_8_5_1_hotfix_grant_rls_helpers.sql  Phase 5.8.5.1 hotfix: GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.is_admin() / public.is_producer_or_admin() / public.current_user_role() TO authenticated. Re-instates EXECUTE on the 3 RLS helpers that the prior migration (20260531160000) REVOKE'd FROM PUBLIC without re-GRANTing on the assumption that SQL-function inlining would skip the permission check. Wrong assumption: SECURITY DEFINER blocks inlining, and every RLS predicate caller needs EXECUTE. Production TS open-roles list went empty within seconds of the 5.8.5 push; hotfix GRANT applied via Supabase Dashboard SQL editor 2026-05-18 restored production immediately. GRANT is idempotent; this migration is a no-op against prod (the dashboard hotfix already granted these) but registers in supabase_migrations.schema_migrations so any future supabase db reset / fresh rebuild from migrations re-applies the fix. Post-hotfix advisor count: authenticated_security_definer_function_executable family grows from 4 (5.8.5 carve-outs: credentials_create + credentials_set_password + credentials_reveal_password + promote_outlook_to_project) to 7 (now also includes is_admin + is_producer_or_admin + current_user_role); the 3 new entries are intentional carve-outs documented in docs/decisions.md "RLS helper EXECUTE carve-out". Memory: feedback_revoke_execute_check_rls_callers.md. (APPLIED 2026-05-18)

DO/IF EXISTS guard for rls_auto_enable. 20260521100000_phase_5_6_5_1_owner_column_gate.sql  Phase 5.6.5.1: CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.users_protect_admin_columns() adding a third clause that gates is_owner column writes to owners only. The new clause fires when OLD.is_owner IS DISTINCT FROM NEW.is_owner: first requires the caller to be an owner via inline EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM public.users WHERE id = auth.uid() AND is_owner = true) (raises 'Only owners can change is_owner' otherwise — matches the is_admin() inline-subquery shape from the existing permission_role + active clauses; avoids introducing a separate is_owner() SQL function that would later need policy-dependency audits if dropped). Second clause inside the same IF blocks self-revoke (NEW.id = auth.uid() AND OLD.is_owner = true AND NEW.is_owner = false raises 'Owners cannot revoke their own owner status') so the last-owner-locks-themselves-out failure mode is structurally impossible without an explicit at-least-one-owner guardrail. Function stays SECURITY DEFINER + SET search_path = public; CREATE OR REPLACE keeps the OID-stable binding to trg_users_protect_admin_columns (no DROP, no policy-dep audit risk). No GRANT change. No types regen needed (trigger function bodies don't surface in generated TS); ran as sanity check + produced no diff. Wrapped in BEGIN/COMMIT. (APPLIED 2026-05-17)

20260517100000_phase_5_6_1_phone_normalization.sql           Phase 5.6.1: data-only normalize-existing-rows migration. pg_temp.normalize_phone(raw text) helper extracts exactly 10 US digits via `regexp_replace(raw, '[^0-9]', '', 'g')`, strips a leading 1 for 11-digit inputs, returns the formatted `(XXX) XXX-XXXX` string when it lands on exactly 10 digits, else passes the raw value through unchanged (international, extensions, garbage all survive). Three UPDATEs target `people.phone`, `vendors.contact_phone`, `clients.contact_phone` with a WHERE clause skipping rows that already match `^\(\d{3}\) \d{3}-\d{4}$` (idempotent + safe to re-run). pg_temp function is session-scoped + auto-drops after the migration transaction. No schema change, no GRANT/RLS impact, no types regen delta. Backs the `formatPhone` save-time-only onBlur handler shipped on PersonEdit + VendorEdit + ClientEdit; existing rows get caught up at migration push so the UI never has to retroactively migrate user data. (APPLIED 2026-05-17)

(APPLIED; pipeline_error rename via 20260514000001 in Phase 4.10.3-port)

(APPLIED)

The nine `phase_4_*` migrations that landed on `main` between Phase 4.1 (Scout Dashboard) and Phase 4.6 (Deck Prep) were repaired to `reverted` in the remote `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations` table on 2026-05-12 ahead of the Phase 4.1-port push. The actual table state is now whatever the port migration produced, regardless of the abandoned history.

**Carried-forward cleanup queued (from cutover):**
- **vs-research-venues duplicate-invocation race.** CAS guards mask the symptom but the underlying race is real. Proper fix: Postgres advisory lock OR kickoff CAS on `brief_data.research_started_at`. Not blocking; both invocations produce valid scouts, just double-spend.
- **`MAX_PAUSE_CONTINUATIONS=1` cap on `callClaude`.** Conservative. If "no structured output" failures surface in prod, raise to 2-3 with a wall-clock budget instead of a continuation-count budget.
- **Real-cron test** of `ts-cron-scheduled-pulls` + watchdogs in production (requires GUCs set in Supabase SQL editor). Tied to the Phase 3.8 production wiring above.
- **Run `to_regclass('public.vs_briefs')` / `vs_sourcing_rounds` / `vs_pitch_decks` in Supabase Studio** to explicit-confirm the 4.1-port migration's drops landed (migration ledger says applied; visual confirmation in Studio is the belt-and-suspenders check).

## How to update this file

Update on every meaningful merge to `main`:
1. Bump **Last updated** to today.
2. Bump **Latest commit on main** to the new HEAD hash + message.
3. Add the new commits to **Recent commits** (keep last 5).
4. Add new migrations to **Recent migrations** if any.
5. Move items between "What's live" / "What's NOT live yet" if behavior changed.
6. Add to "Known issues / drift" anything that needs a future cleanup pass.
7. Adjust **Current phase** + **Next up** when phase boundaries cross.
